```python
number_of_times = []
for crime in a:
    number_of_times.append(((data.loc[data['Primary Type'] == crime]).shape)[0])
print(number_of_times)


```

    [699039, 187129, 1359322, 305219, 746244, 67694, 402886, 1186998, 400018, 243837, 43030, 377341, 246793, 13955, 25459, 65772, 14226, 46576, 13811, 10830, 8890, 23946, 3786, 23, 6515, 3185, 149, 123, 492, 130, 36, 151, 38, 6, 1]



```python

data.loc[data['Primary Type'] == 'HOMICIDE' & (data['YEAR' == 2008)]
```
